DO NOT GET VACCINATIONS AT WALGREENS!

So, last week I found that I could make online appointments for vaccinations at Walgreens (for the Philippines trip). I did all of the online stuff, then called our local store, talked to a pharmacist to check prices and availability and confirmed the appointment.

We went in today, exactly on time for the appointment, and the girl at the window told us we didn't need an appointment and that she'd be happy to take care of my shots. All she needed was my list of what we needed.

I had left that at home, because in making the appointment, I told online Walgreens exactly what I needed.

We sat for 20 minutes while the girl took a quick course on computer use, then applied her knowledge to find the information about my appointment on the magical glowing box near the register.  Smiling, she finally could take care of me... or not.

Predictably, they had nothing that I needed except tetanus boosters. She said that typhoid vaccine was nonexistent, and she'd have to order the others and that it would be weeks before I could get my shots.

That was when I stormed out rather than scream at the poor girl and inspire someone to call the cops.

When I got home, I found a nearby clinic that could give me all the shots I needed--including the supposedly nonexistent typhoid shot--right away.  It costs a bit more, but I'll gladly pay to avoid the headache of ever having to step into this crappy Walgreens again.</Text>

< Rate>
3<//Rate>
< review>
While Select is the Physical Therapy place of choice for many collegiate and professional athletes, it's tough to recommend it for regular people.

At most physical therapy places, you work with a physical therapist at a maximum 2:1 patient to PT ratio. It's reasonable to have a physical therapist work with two people at the same time. At Select, after a thorough first meeting with "your" PT, you'll realize that you're splitting time with "your" PT with four or five other patients at the same time.

Because I am fine working independently, it didn't bother me much, but it's certainly not for everyone. It's hard to ignore tall of the discouraged faces that are bummed out from not getting the 1:1 attention that they thought they signed up for.

If you want to be left alone and do some reps and stuff on your own time, Select is worth a look. If you want 1:1 attention, this is not your spot.< /review>

Today was the worse day so far coming to this restaurant!!  I heard from friends the food was good.  I was hesitant at first because it looks so dirty outside.  Because their own were eating here I figured it's good.  It's always busy.

The food is good with the exception of the sweet and sour pork.  The parts that have most of the batter are pork fat underneath.  The parts that look thicker are the same batter fried too much.  The rest of the food I have to say is pretty good.  Today I ordered 3 items and they gave me the nasty sweet and sour pork I don't like instead of my pork fried rice.

<username>Steph Wong<//username><pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNNJzdH4N-ML0QpoJ6Yw-C2y8VkILiHSNXhcn3O=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNfPsWpk8I5QNJoKoqbyfkqeGCLG3el4bBwX716=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNOlZjj4NmWkj-gbq1sJs8TnRxW37wEpt8fzs-g=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]<//pictures><UserId.>113667988363130639473< /UserId.>< GmapID>

<rate>4</rate>< Review>
Tiny hole in the wall spot on Mission. you could probably drive by it and not even notice. Definitely seems like a family-run operation.

Although small their menu is pretty extensive. came here on a Friday night and luckily we came at the time we did. After we sat down it seemed like a rush of people came and the entire restaurant was full.

We ordered four dishes. One of my absolute favorite dishes, hung tao yee fu wonton, was fantastic! The combination of crispy wontons and flavorful soup was perfect. Definitely something you should order. Next up was salt and pepper porkchops. Nicely fried and very crispy. We got two vegetable dishes. The eggplant was very good. We also got pea sprouts. Unfortunately I didn't eat them because I was way too full, but my parents said they were good!

Although this is a small restaurant, this place provides huge portions for what they charge. I suggest coming early so you don't have to wait.</Review>

< Text>
You will wait a long time. You can't expect fancy service or decor.

It's outstanding, homestyle chinese, at a low price. The wontons and eggrolls, even spring rolls are freshly homemade and it shows. They feature fried smelts, and various classics. The chinese broccoli and greens are flavorful and never overcooked.  The food is made to order. The quality and portions are generous.

It confuses me when people complain about decor and service in a place that is obviously just a takeout - and a very busy one at that because of it's loyal following. Get the food here. You won't be dissapointed.</Text>

< text>
Between Panera and Coldstone.   The Starbucks app and website label this location as 'Roosevelt & Rosecrans' but it is in Liberty Station on Truxton Rd.  I understand there is another Starbucks inside Vons in the same plaza (I cannot confirm as I do not shop there).  This however, is a stand alone location and always has high traffic.  The staff is almost always wonderful, seem to know their local folks and are good about acknowledging regular faces.  It is tiny inside but there are 7-8 very small tables and a bar that will seat 2 comfortably.  About 4-5 outlets as far as I can tell.  I've been here a dozen times during my 3 month visit to the area and I have always managed to find a table with an outlet within a short time of arriving (if not immediately).<//text>
